 pulavama atake (pulwama Attack) ke baad bhartiya vayusena (indian Air Force) ne pakistan (pakistan) main ghuskar jaish-e-mohammad (jaish-e-mohammed) ke aatanki thikaanon par air strike kii thi
 On February 26, 12 Mirage crossed the Pakistani airspace while flying from several air bases and carried out a missile attack on jaish-e-mohammed's terrorist camp in Balakot city of Khyber Pakhtunwa province
 bhartiya air force ke wing commander amit ranjan, swarden leader rahul basoya, pankaj bhujaade, bikeen reddy, shashaank singh ne jaish-e-mohammad ke aatanki camp (jaish-e-mohammed terrorist camp) ko dhwast kiya tha
 He will now be given the Air Force Medal
 Indian Air Force's Wg Cdr Amit Ranjan, Sqn Ldrs Rahul Basoya, Pankaj Bhujade, BKN Reddy, Shashank Singh awarded Vayu Sena Medal (gallantry) for bombing jaish-e-mohammed terrorist camp in Pakistan's Balakot town
 All officers are Mirage 2000 fighter aircraft pilots

 jagan mohan reddy kii raajnneetik yatra yaheen se shuru hui
 Before joining politics, Jagan Mohan was a successful businessman
 sirf 27 saal kii hi umr main jagan mohan reddy ne kaarobaar shuru kar diya tha
 The father was the Chief Minister and Jagan Mohan was doing wonders in the business of infrastructure to cement factory and media
 lekin pita kii aakasmik maut ne jagan mohan ko andar se tod diya
 Jagan Mohan hoped that his father had united day and night to strengthen the Congress party in Andhra Pradesh
 unki maut ke baad bete ko party main tarjeeh milegi
 but that did not happen
 jab congress ne nahin maani mangavayiesar kii maut ke baad party vidhayak jagan mohan reddy ko siem banane kii maang karne lage
 But the Congress high command ignored Jagan Mohan
 rosaiyya ko mukhyamantri bana diya
 This was the time when Jagan Mohan had two options, one- he would sit quietly at home after listening to the party, second- he showed courage to walk on a different path by strengthening his father's popularity, Jagan Mohan chose the other way and his father 'YSR Congress' formed a separate party in the name
 congress ne mukhyamantri banane se kar diya tha inkaarwaiesar reddy kii lokapriyata itani thi ki unki maut kii khabar sunakar kai logon ne aatmahatya kar lee thi
 Jagan Mohan was on a state-wide tour to console the people of Andhra
 is yatra ke dauraan jagan mohan unke ghar tak pahunch rahe the jinke parivaar ke sadsy ne aatmahatya kar lee thi
 Actually after the death of his father, Jagan Mohan reached the Congress office with the hope
 lekin party unhen mukhyamantri banane se inkaar kar diya
 After this, Jagan Mohan came out of the Congress office after getting angry and sad
 unhen pita kii maut ke baad rajya main shradhanjali yatra tak nikaalane kii anumati nahin mili thi
 In the middle of 2010, Jagan Mohan Reddy's mother Vijayalakshmi (vijayamma) arrived at 10 Janpath to meet Sonia Gandhi with her daughter Sharmila Reddy after Jagan Mohan
 kaha jaataa he ki wiesar reddy or rajeev gandhi ke bich kaaphi ghanishtha sambandh the, jisase vijayalakshmi ko ummid thi ki sonia gandhi unki baat ko gambhirtha se lengi
 But when he had to wait long to meet the then President of Congress, all his hopes were shattered
 vijaymma chaahati thim ki jagan mohan ko party main koi sammanjanak pad mili
 But when he met Sonia Gandhi, the Congress President told him that first of all you ask Jagan Mohan to stop the journey
 jagan mohan reddy kaa kahana he ki congress daftar main unke baad unki maa-bahan kaa bhi apmaan kiya gaya
 To avenge this, he formed a separate party
 bahan ke saath jagan mohan reddy
 The 18 Congress mlas left the party and joined Jagan Mohan after the formation of the first successful BYSR Congress in the 2012 by-election
 jiske baad in 18 siton par 2012 main up-chunaav hue
 In this by-election, Jagan Mohan's party shocked everyone and won 15 of the 18 seats
 iske baad jagan mohan reddy lagaataar andhra pradesh kii raajnneeti main apni jagah banane ke liye sangharsh karte rahe
 During this, he had to go to jail
 16 maheene tak rahe jail mendrasal saal 2003 main jahaan jagan mohan kii sampatti kareeb 10 lakh rupee thi, vahiin 2011 main apane pita kii seat kadappa se chunaav ladate hue die halafname main unki sampatti badhkar 300 karod rupee ho gai
 After which a Congress minister and 2 TDP leaders filed a petition against Jagan Mohan in the High Court and then on the orders of the High Court, the CBI got involved in the investigation
 iske alaava aay se adhik sampatti maamle main jagan ke khilaaf idi or inakam tex kii jaanch chal rahi thi
 During the investigation, Jagan Mohan Reddy was arrested
 kareeb 16 maheene tak jagan mohan reddy jail main rahe
 Now Jagan Mohan reached the public again after Jagan Mohan's departure from the Taj
 chandrababu naidu sarkaar ke khilaaf padayatra shuru kar di

 2019 ke rigelt ke saath hi reddy kii saughandh bhi puri ho gai he

 unhone apni schuli shiksha hyderabad public skool se puri kii

 unhone bi

 desh nyaay maang rahaa he
